could do it better than anybodi els be acquaint with all pirat crew in that ocean and though it would take him a long time to get there without money he would get there anyway and everi time he convinc a pirat he would say to him dont you thank me dont you give me no credit it all belong to them dear peopl in pokevill camp meet natur brother and benefactor of the race and that dear preacher busi and one minut you could see everyth and everi face in that big crowd and the shovel of dirt sail up out of the grave and the next second the dark wipe it all out and you couldnt see noth at all couldnt prop it up right and she would alway cave in  but of cours we thought of the right way at lastwhich was to cook the ladder too in the pie  so then we laid in with jim the second night and tore up the sheet all in littl string and twist them togeth and long befor daylight we had a love rope that you could a hung a person with  we let on it took nine month to make it and in the forenoon we took it down to the wood but it wouldnt go into the pie  be made of a whole sheet that way there was rope enough for forti pie if wed a want them and plenti left over for soup or sausag or anyth you choos  we could a had a whole dinner but we didnt need it  all we need was just enough for the pie and so we throw the rest away  we didnt cook none of the pie in the wash panafraid the solder would relict you know and we snake her out privat and took her down there but she fail on the first pie becaus we didnt know how but she come up smile on the last one  we took and line her with dough and set her in the coal and load her up with rag rope and put on a dough roof and shut down the lid and put hot ember on top and stood off five foot with the long handl cool and comfort and in fifteen minut she turn out a pie that was a satisfact to look at but the person that et it would want to fetch a coupl of kag of toothpick along for if that rope ladder wouldnt cramp him down to busi i dont throw it out of the window hole chapter xxxviii make them pen was a distressid tough job and so was the saw and jim allow the inscript was go to be the toughest of all  that the one which the prison manag to set a nigger free that was alreadi free befor and he said what he had plan in his head from the start if we got jim out all safe was for us to run him down the river on the raft and have adventur plumb to the mouth of the river and then tell him about his be free and take him back up home on a steamboat in style and pay him for his lost time and write word ahead and get out all the nigger around and have them waltz him into town with a torchlight process and a brass band and then he would be a hero and so would we  but i reckon it was about as well the way it was we had jim out of the chain in no time and when aunt polli and uncl sila and aunt salli found out how good he help the doctor nurs tom they made a heap of fuss over him and fix him up prime and give him all he want to eat and a good time and noth to do  and we had him up to the sick room and had a high talk and tom give jim forti dollar for be prison for us so patient and do it up so good and jim was pleas most to death and bust out and say dah now huck what i tell youwhat i tell you up dah on jackson islan  i tole you i got a hairi brea en what de sign un it en i tole you i ben rich wunst en gwinet to be rich agin en it come true en heah she is Â  dah now doan talk to me sign is sign mine i tell you en i know jis s well at i uz gwinet be rich agin as is a stannin heah dis minut and then tom he talk along and talk along and say les all three slide out of here one of these night and get an outfit and go for howl adventur amongst the injun over in the territori for a coupl of week or two and i say all right that suit me but i aint got no money for to buy the outfit and i reckon i couldnt get none from home becaus it like pap been back befor now and got it all away from judg thatcher and drunk it up no he haint tom say it all there yetsix thousand dollar and more and your pap haint ever been back sinc  hadnt when i come away anyhow jim say kind of solemn he aint a comin back no mo huck i say whi jim nemmin whi huckbut he aint comin back no mo but i kept at him so at last he say doan you member de hous dat was floatn down de river en dey wuz a man in dah kiver up en i went in en unkiv him and didn let you come in  well den you kin git yo money when you want it kase dat wuz him tom most well now and got his bullet around his neck on a watch guard for a watch and is alway see what time it is and so there aint noth more to write about and i am rotten glad of it becaus if id a know what a troubl it was to make a book i wouldnt a tackl it and aint a go to no more  but i reckon i got to light out for the territori ahead of the rest becaus aunt salli shes go to adopt me and sivil me and i cant stand it  i been there befor the end your truli huck finn
